    <td style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);word-break:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;padding-left:0.042in;vertical-align:top;"><p style="text-indent:0.0pt;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.05;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"></span>&#160;</p></td>
    <td style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);word-break:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;padding-left:0.042in;vertical-align:top;"><p style="text-indent:0.0pt;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.05;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"></span>&#160;</p></td>
    <td style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);word-break:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;padding-left:0.042in;vertical-align:bottom;"><p style="text-indent:0.0pt;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.05;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"></span>&#160;</p></td>
    <td style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);word-break:break-word;white-space:pre-wrap;padding-left:0.042in;vertical-align:bottom;padding-right:0.028in;"><p style="text-indent:0.0pt;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.05;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><span style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">President and Chief Executive Officer</span></p></td>

  <title>EX-99.1</title>
 </head>
 <body>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:right;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Exhibit 99.1</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><img src="img247042425_0.jpg" alt="img247042425_0.jpg" style="width:174px;height:86px;">&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Athira Pharma Reports Second Quarter 2022 Financial Results and Recent Clinical and Corporate Updates</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Presented clinical and preclinical data at Alzheimer&#x2019;s Association International Conference 2022</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Strong balance sheet to support clinical development pipeline</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">BOTHELL, WA, August 15, 2022</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"> &#x2014; </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Athira Pharma, Inc.</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"> (NASDAQ: ATHA), a late clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company focused on developing small molecules to restore neuronal health and slow neurodegeneration, today announced the company&#x2019;s financial results for the second quarter ended June 30, 2022 and reviewed recent clinical and corporate updates.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"> </font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">&#x201c;We are encouraged by the biologic activity and safety topline results from the ACT-AD trial in Alzheimer&#x2019;s disease. While the primary endpoint did not reach statistical significance, the trial results are the first ever to show potential cognitive improvement through positive modulation of the HGF/MET receptor by fosgonimeton. This is an important achievement supporting our conviction that we have a unique opportunity to reshape the course of neurodegenerative diseases,&#x201d; stated Mark Litton, Ph.D., President and Chief Executive Officer of Athira.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">&#x201c;The growing body of clinical and preclinical data with fosgonimeton and our other novel HGF/MET positive modulators support the potential for this pathway to improve neuronal health in a number of neurodegenerative diseases.  Importantly, we are pleased to have a strong balance sheet that can support our programs through a number of key inflection points,&#x201d; concluded Dr. Litton.</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Clinical Update:</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Fosgonimeton (ATH-1017)</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"> is a small molecule specifically designed to enhance the activity of Hepatocyte Growth Factor (HGF) and its receptor, MET.</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:3.333%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:13.5pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">ACT-AD Phase 2 Study in mild-to-moderate Alzheimer&#x2019;s disease (</font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">NCT04491006</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">)</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Announced topline results in June 2022 from the proof-of-concept ACT-AD Phase 2 study of fosgonimeton (ATH-1017) in patients with mild-to-moderate Alzheimer&#x2019;s disease (AD). </font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:10.0%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.7033333333333336%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">The study did not meet the primary endpoint of a statistically significant change in event related potential (ERP) P300 latency for the protocoled modified intent to treat (mITT) population by a mixed model repeated measures (MMRM) analysis (-6.02 milliseconds) when compared with placebo at 26 weeks in a pooled analysis of the 40 mg and 70 mg dose groups. </font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:10.0%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.7033333333333336%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">A post hoc analysis, based on the mITT population on fosgonimeton monotherapy, showed potentially beneficial, but not statistically significant, changes in ERP P300 latency compared to placebo at 26 weeks (-28 milliseconds) as well as cognitive </font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <div style="margin-left:10.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;visibility:hidden;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.7033333333333336%;"></font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">improvement as measured by ADAS-Cog11 (-3.3 points) compared with placebo at 26 weeks.</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Additional data from the ACT-AD Phase 2 study were presented in August 2022 at the Alzheimer's Association International Conference 2022 (AAIC 2022) by Hans Moebius, M.D., Ph.D., Athira&#x2019;s Chief Medical Officer.  Highlights of the additional data showed:</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:10.0%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.7033333333333336%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">A numerical, but not statistically significant, improvement in the functional measure of ADCS-ADL23, a secondary endpoint which evaluates improvements in patients&#x2019; activities of daily living as assessed by their caregivers, compared to placebo at 26 weeks in the protocoled mITT population by MMRM analysis (+2.12 points, n.s.).</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:10.0%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.7033333333333336%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">A statistically significant improvement in plasma levels of neurofilament light chain (NfL), a validated fluid biomarker of neurodegeneration, in a prespecified subgroup of subjects treated with fosgonimeton monotherapy compared with placebo at 26 weeks (difference of 6.89 pg/ml (p=0.018)), and showed a numerical, but not statistically significant, improvement in all fosgonimeton treated patients compared with placebo at 26 weeks (difference of 1.67 pg/ml), regardless of background therapy. </font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">The ACT-AD trial was supported by a grant from the National Institute on Aging of the National Institutes of Health under Award Number R01AG06268. The information presented in this press release is solely the responsibility of Athira and does not necessarily represent the official views of the National Institutes of Health.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:3.333%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:13.5pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">LIFT-AD Phase 3 Study in mild-to-moderate Alzheimer&#x2019;s Disease (</font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">NCT04488419</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">)</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Recruitment in the LIFT-AD trial is ongoing, with over 300 patients enrolled to-date.</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">With feedback from its Scientific Advisory Board and the Data Safety Monitoring Board, Athira continues to evaluate the best next steps for the LIFT-AD trial.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:3.333%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Open Label Extension Study (</font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">NCT04886063</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">)</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">In May 2022, Athira extended its Open Label Extension (OLEX) study for the ACT-AD and LIFT-AD studies to up to 18 months following the completion of the 26-week treatment period in the ACT-AD or LIFT-AD study. </font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">As of August 2022, more than 90 percent of patients who have completed the LIFT-AD and ACT-AD studies have elected to participate in the OLEX study.</font></div></div>
  <p style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:13.5pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">SHAPE Phase 2 Study in Parkinson&#x2019;s disease dementia and Dementia with Lewy bodies (</font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">NCT04831281</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">)</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Athira dosed the first patient in the SHAPE trial in January 2022. SHAPE is a randomized, double-blind, placebo-controlled, parallel-group Phase 2 proof-of-concept study of fosgonimeton in approximately 75 participants with Parkinson&#x2019;s disease dementia or Dementia with Lewy bodies.</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Recruitment is ongoing.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:13.5pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">ATH-1020 </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">is an orally available, brain-penetrant small molecule designed to enhance the HGF/MET system that is being advanced as a potential treatment candidate for neuropsychiatric indications.</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:3.333%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:13.5pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Phase 1 Study in Healthy Volunteers (</font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">NCT05169671</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">)</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">In the first quarter of 2022, Athira initiated a Phase 1 study to evaluate the safety, tolerability, and pharmacokinetics of ATH-1020 in approximately 68 healthy young and elderly volunteers.</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Dose escalation is ongoing.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:13.5pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Research and Development Update:</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Preclinical Data Presented at </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Alzheimer's Association International Conference 2022</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Data from a poster titled, &#x201c;Fosgonimeton, a novel, small molecule positive modulator of the HGF/MET system is neuroprotective in primary neuron culture,&#x201d; demonstrated that fosgo-AM, the active metabolite of Athira&#x2019;s lead pipeline candidate, fosgonimeton (ATH-1017), promotes neurotrophic effects and offers protection against neurological insults implicated in mitochondrial dysfunction, excitotoxicity, inflammation and oxidative stress central to neurodegeneration. These neuroprotective effects highlight the therapeutic potential for fosgonimeton to restore neuronal health and slow neurodegeneration. </font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Data from a poster titled, &#x201c;Development of stable, orally bioavailable small molecule positive modulators of HGF/MET signaling for the treatment of cognitive impairment,&#x201d; focused on the identification and preclinical validation of a panel of novel, small molecule HGF/MET positive modulators. These orally bioavailable molecules significantly reversed scopolamine-induced spatial memory deficits in rats. They also demonstrated favorable pharmacokinetics, including efficient distribution to the brain following administration. Based on these promising preclinical data, Athira intends to continue developing these compounds for the potential treatment of Alzheimer&#x2019;s disease and other neurodegenerative disorders.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Preclinical Data Presented at Peripheral Nerve Society (PNS) 2022 Annual Meeting</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Athira presented new data at the PNS 2022 Annual Meeting in a poster presentation titled, &#x201c;Small Molecule HGF/MET Positive Modulator Effectively Reduces Pain-Related Behaviors in a Rat Diabetic Neuropathy Model.&#x201d;  The data are supportive of the HGF/MET mechanism and the company&#x2019;s future plans to investigate its potential in a peripheral nerve application.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Corporate Update:</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">In June 2022, Athira announced the formation of a Scientific Advisory Board (SAB) comprised of renowned leaders in neurology research, including John Olichney, M.D., Anton Porsteinsson, M.D., Marwan Sabbagh, M.D., Lon Schneider, M.D., Pierre Tariot, M.D., and Paul Winner, M.D. The SAB is chaired by Dr. Moebius, Athira&#x2019;s Chief Medical Officer, and provides expert scientific and clinical perspectives to guide the ongoing development of Athira&#x2019;s pipeline of novel, small molecule compounds.</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">In May 2022, Athira announced stockholder approval of the election of its independent director nominees to the company&#x2019;s board of directors: Joseph Edelman, John M. Fluke, Jr. and Grant Pickering.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Financial Results</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Cash Position</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">. Cash, cash equivalents and investments were $282.2 million as of June 30, 2022, compared with $319.7 million as of December 31, 2021. Cash used in operations was $35.2 million for the six months ended June 30, 2022, compared with $14.6 million for the six months ended June 30, 2021.<br></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Research and Development (R&amp;D) Expenses</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">. R&amp;D expenses were $14.8 million for the quarter ended June 30, 2022, compared with $12.0 million for the same period in 2021. The increase was driven primarily by costs related to increased clinical trial activities, expanded personnel, </font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;visibility:hidden;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;"></font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">and increased preclinical research and development expenses.  <br></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">General and Administrative (G&amp;A) Expenses. </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">G&amp;A expenses were $8.8 million for the quarter ended June 30, 2022, compared with $4.6 million for same period in 2021. The change was primarily due to increased personnel expense as the company&#x2019;s headcount expanded to support its continued growth. In addition, increases to G&amp;A expenses in 2022 were the result of costs associated with legal proceedings and the proxy contest in connection with the company&#x2019;s 2022 annual stockholders meeting. </font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Net Loss</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">. The company reported a net loss of $24.3 million, or $0.65 per share, for the second quarter ended June 30, 2022, compared with a net loss of $14.0 million, or $0.38 per share, for the second quarter ended June 30, 2021. </font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">About Athira Pharma, Inc.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Athira Pharma, Inc., headquartered in the Seattle area, is a late clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company focused on developing small molecules to restore neuronal health and slow neurodegeneration. Athira aims to provide rapid cognitive improvement and alter the course of neurological diseases with its novel mechanism of action. Athira is currently advancing its lead therapeutic candidate, fosgonimeton, a novel small molecule for Alzheimer&#x2019;s and Parkinson&#x2019;s disease dementia and Dementia with Lewy bodies. For more information, visit </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">www.athira.com</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">. You can also follow Athira on </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Facebook</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">, </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">LinkedIn</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"> and @athirapharma on </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Twitter</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;"> and </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">Instagram</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></p>

if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
